       <li class="devsite-nav-item devsite-nav-item-section-expandable devsite-nav-accordion"><span class="devsite-nav-title devsite-nav-title-no-path" track-type="leftNav" track-name="expandNavSectionNoLink" track-metadata-position="0">Dynamic Links</span><a class="devsite-nav-toggle devsite-nav-toggle-collapsed material-icons" track-type="leftNav" track-name="expandNavSectionArrow" track-metadata-position="0"></a>
        <ul class="devsite-nav-section devsite-nav-section-collapsed">
         <li class="devsite-nav-item"><a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/dynamic-links/" class="devsite-nav-title gc-analytics-event" track-type="leftNav" track-name="titleLink" track-metadata-position="1" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Left nav" data-action="click">Introduction</a></li>
         <li class="devsite-nav-item devsite-nav-item-section-expandable"><span class="devsite-nav-title devsite-nav-title-no-path" track-type="leftNav" track-name="expandNavSectionNoLink" track-metadata-position="1">Use Cases</span><a class="devsite-nav-toggle devsite-nav-toggle-collapsed material-icons" track-type="leftNav" track-name="expandNavSectionArrow" track-metadata-position="1"></a>
          <ul class="devsite-nav-section devsite-nav-section-collapsed">
           <li class="devsite-nav-item"><a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/dynamic-links/use-cases/" class="devsite-nav-title gc-analytics-event" track-type="leftNav" track-name="titleLink" track-metadata-position="2" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Left nav" data-action="click">Overview</a></li>
           <li class="devsite-nav-item"><a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/dynamic-links/use-cases/web-to-app" class="devsite-nav-title gc-analytics-event" track-type="leftNav" track-name="titleLink" track-metadata-position="2" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Left nav" data-action="click">Convert Web Users To App Users</a></li>

       <nav class="devsite-breadcrumb-nav devsite-nav"> 
        <ul class="devsite-breadcrumb-list"> 
         <li class="devsite-breadcrumb-item"> <a href="https://firebase.google.com/" class="devsite-breadcrumb-link gc-analytics-event" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Breadcrumbs" data-value="1"> Firebase </a> </li> 
         <li class="devsite-breadcrumb-item"> 
          <div class="devsite-breadcrumb-guillemet material-icons"></div> <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/" class="devsite-breadcrumb-link gc-analytics-event" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Breadcrumbs" data-value="2"> Docs </a> </li> 
         <li class="devsite-breadcrumb-item"> 
          <div class="devsite-breadcrumb-guillemet material-icons"></div> <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/guides/" class="devsite-breadcrumb-link gc-analytics-event" data-category="Site-Wide Custom Events" data-label="Breadcrumbs" data-value="3"> Guides </a> </li> 
        </ul> 
       </nav> 
       <h1 itemprop="name" class="devsite-page-title"> Authenticate with Firebase using Password-Based Accounts using Javascript </h1> 
       <nav class="devsite-page-nav-embedded devsite-nav"></nav> 
       <div class="devsite-article-body clearfix
            " itemprop="articleBody"> 
        <p>You can use Firebase Authentication to let your users authenticate with Firebase using their email addresses and passwords, and to manage your app's password-based accounts.</p> 
        <h2 id="before_you_begin">Before you begin</h2> 
        <ol> 
         <li><a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/web/setup">Add Firebase to your JavaScript project</a>. </li>
         <li>If you haven't yet connected your app to your Firebase project, do so from the <a href="//console.firebase.google.com/" class="link external gc-analytics-event" data-category="console" data-action="linkClick">Firebase console</a>.</li> 
         <li>Enable Email/Password sign-in: 
          <ol> 
           <li>In the <a href="//console.firebase.google.com/" class="link external gc-analytics-event" data-category="console" data-action="linkClick">Firebase console</a>, open the <b>Auth</b> section.</li> 
           <li>On the <b>Sign in method</b> tab, enable the <b>Email/password</b> sign-in method and click <b>Save</b>.</li> 
          </ol> </li>  
        </ol> 
        <h2 id="create_a_password-based_account">Create a password-based account</h2> 
        <p>To create a new user account with a password, complete the following steps in your app's sign-up page:</p> 
        <ol> 
         <li>When a new user signs up using your app's sign-up form, complete any new account validation steps that your app requires, such as verifying that the new account's password was correctly typed and meets your complexity requirements.</li> 
         <li>Create a new account by passing the new user's email address and password to <code>createUserWithEmailAndPassword</code>: <pre class="prettyprint">firebase.auth().createUserWithEmailAndPassword(email, password).catch(function(error) {
  // Handle Errors here.
  var errorCode = error.code;
  var errorMessage = error.message;
  // ...
});</pre> If the new account was created, the user is signed in automatically. Have a look at the Next steps section below to get the signed in user details. <p> This is also where you can catch and handle errors. For a list of error codes have a look at the <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/reference/js/firebase.auth.Auth#createUserWithEmailAndPassword">Auth Reference Docs</a>. </p> </li> 
        </ol> 
        <aside>
         To protect your project from abuse, Firebase limits the number of new email/password and anonymous sign-ups that your application can have from the same IP address in a short period of time. You can request and schedule temporary changes to this quota from the 
         <a href="//console.firebase.google.com/project/_/authentication/providers" class="link external">Firebase console</a>.
        </aside> 
        <h2 id="sign_in_a_user_with_an_email_address_and_password">Sign in a user with an email address and password</h2> 
        <p>The steps for signing in a user with a password are similar to the steps for creating a new account. In your app's sign-in page, do the following:</p> 
        <ol> 
         <li>When a user signs in to your app, pass the user's email address and password to <code>signInWithEmailAndPassword</code>: <pre class="prettyprint">firebase.auth().signInWithEmailAndPassword(email, password).catch(function(error) {
  // Handle Errors here.
  var errorCode = error.code;
  var errorMessage = error.message;
  // ...
});</pre> Have a look at the Next steps section below to get the signed in user details. <p> This is also where you can catch and handle errors. For a list of error codes have a look at the <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/reference/js/firebase.auth.Auth#signInWithEmailAndPassword">Auth Reference Docs</a>. </p> </li> 
        </ol> 
        <h2 id="next_steps">Next steps</h2> 
        <p>After a user signs in for the first time, a new user account is created and linked to the credentialsthat is, the user name and password, phone number, or auth provider informationthe user signed in with. This new account is stored as part of your Firebase project, and can be used to identify a user across every app in your project, regardless of how the user signs in. </p> 
        <ul> 
         <li> <p>In your apps, the recommended way to know the auth status of your user is to set an observer on the <code>Auth</code> object. You can then get the user's basic profile information from the <code>User</code> object. See <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/auth/web/manage-users">Manage Users</a>.</p> </li> 
         <li><p>In your Firebase Realtime Database and Cloud Storage <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/database/security/user-security">Security Rules</a>, you can get the signed-in user's unique user ID from the <code>auth</code> variable, and use it to control what data a user can access.</p></li> 
        </ul> 
        <p>You can allow users to sign in to your app using multiple authentication providers by <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/auth/web/account-linking">linking auth provider credentials to an existing user account.</a></p> 
        <p>To sign out a user, call <a href="https://firebase.google.com/docs/reference/js/firebase.auth.Auth.html#signOut"> <code>signOut</code></a>:</p> 
        <pre class="prettyprint">
firebase.auth().signOut().then(function() {
  // Sign-out successful.
}).catch(function(error) {
  // An error happened.
});
</pre> 
       </div>
